if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access') != '28f4ba83265894b08c5084e8fdbbbd83108ebb75') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access') !== '28f4ba83265894b08c5084e8fdbbbd83108ebb75') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access') !== '62660fe35f5ccb033ef3d5b8951bd8ce7f04fc2c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_access') !== '28f4ba83265894b08c5084e8fdbbbd83108ebb75') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_access');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql') != 'fb3a6624d048400c3e4c5f91f3ff27f746cc8dae') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql') !== 'fb3a6624d048400c3e4c5f91f3ff27f746cc8dae') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql') !== '3290dcfe1634802656662a57bdfcca6828c2fead') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql') !== 'fb3a6624d048400c3e4c5f91f3ff27f746cc8dae') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mssql');
		}
	}
}

} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') !== 'bfd2a0e16701b8230c921882c8f05570b21584e6') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') !== '7c01dbbb9ee5e051a12de4bb670e308db7905328') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql') !== 'bfd2a0e16701b8230c921882c8f05570b21584e6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_mysql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql') != '971a7cfa95431b5d754802ce92e4020510891202') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql') !== '971a7cfa95431b5d754802ce92e4020510891202') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql') !== '9be14b1a8d55ff4ada202ac4af280db9c085a7ed') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql') !== '971a7cfa95431b5d754802ce92e4020510891202') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_pgsql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite') != '0b299a4228fc55ee7db7bbc60e86e95729fb4840') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite') !== '0b299a4228fc55ee7db7bbc60e86e95729fb4840') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite') !== '07dd30456755178044b3fa05a30775b45fe0369d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite') !== '0b299a4228fc55ee7db7bbc60e86e95729fb4840') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
		}
	}
}

		}
		writefile_13();

			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/oidinfo_add_missing');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/recanonize_ids');
	writefile_18();
	if (!is_file('dev/recanonize_ids')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/recanonize_ids');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/recanonize_ids') != '3662aa6f1ad0b7cfc804593e162f05ef5af31e1d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/recanonize_ids');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/recanonize_ids', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/recanonize_ids');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/recanonize_ids') !== '3662aa6f1ad0b7cfc804593e162f05ef5af31e1d') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/recanonize_ids') !== '6b1a9fcdcee4f0979c7c18b5121f659dc904d027') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/recanonize_ids');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/recanonize_ids');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/recanonize_ids')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/recanonize_ids', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/recanonize_ids') !== '3662aa6f1ad0b7cfc804593e162f05ef5af31e1d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/recanonize_ids');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/test_database_plugins')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/test_database_plugins');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('dev/test_database_plugins')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test_database_plugins');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') != 'b84a814855bcfc7caa051d90ce47b17ea648558b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test_database_plugins');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test_database_plugins', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test_database_plugins');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') !== 'b84a814855bcfc7caa051d90ce47b17ea648558b') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') !== 'b86455184be2b97d74ae49ee7fe61ca2c7fe3eeb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test_database_plugins');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test_database_plugins');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test_database_plugins')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/test_database_plugins', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') !== 'b84a814855bcfc7caa051d90ce47b17ea648558b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/test_database_plugins');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/test_logmasks')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/test_logmasks');
	writefile_21();
	if (!is_file('dev/test_logmasks')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test_logmasks');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') != '0d10c865e5e95317bd9b265415ec67ca8eac9d49') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test_logmasks');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test_logmasks', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test_logmasks');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') !== '0d10c865e5e95317bd9b265415ec67ca8eac9d49') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') !== '882726b245cf3a4d81ff832a417660d32780f914') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test_logmasks');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test_logmasks');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test_logmasks')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/test_logmasks', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_21();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') !== '0d10c865e5e95317bd9b265415ec67ca8eac9d49') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/test_logmasks');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	writefile_22();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') != '7db716f8cdddb24c646d9d10f88157a7845a76c1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') !== '7db716f8cdddb24c646d9d10f88157a7845a76c1') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') !== '646098701a988ca29c60e10c348e8cf9c5b81585') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_22();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps') !== '7db716f8cdddb24c646d9d10f88157a7845a76c1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/generate_proof_files.phps');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	writefile_23();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') != '3f9d93c57fa747b511b453815eb69af48fdb1e2d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '3f9d93c57fa747b511b453815eb69af48fdb1e2d') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '7b8b5a21e17f2ee9a28cb90f4bb0d45b19885818') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_23();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '3f9d93c57fa747b511b453815eb69af48fdb1e2d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	writefile_24();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') != 'b5f8cc2ac1c58aa0fcad0d9dbacad3bacdb0ba99') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') !== 'b5f8cc2ac1c58aa0fcad0d9dbacad3bacdb0ba99') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') !== '751c8999e9fa48d87e14eb06ac5403bf3f14e479') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_24();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps') !== 'b5f8cc2ac1c58aa0fcad0d9dbacad3bacdb0ba99') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/show_nontranslated_code.phps');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_25();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != '2cb671077996b4f9367abfd1cb4d78356f661fbb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '2cb671077996b4f9367abfd1cb4d78356f661fbb') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'b7c23d0580804829dc0cf389045e48ed5e2a471d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_25();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '2cb671077996b4f9367abfd1cb4d78356f661fbb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_26();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') != 'b3f8be54cff8a4e7f355fe84517a429b0193e566') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'b3f8be54cff8a4e7f355fe84517a429b0193e566') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '1530ec799c74277718cc426120e9ceabb0eb4f53') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_26();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'b3f8be54cff8a4e7f355fe84517a429b0193e566') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	writefile_27();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') != '14ca1d0d53bf5d497e23c8716bf9b4e3931df819') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '14ca1d0d53bf5d497e23c8716bf9b4e3931df819') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '6aa8b0ef9fd77dcb7d83b1ed47f28077e2df7bf9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_27();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '14ca1d0d53bf5d497e23c8716bf9b4e3931df819') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_29();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php') !== 'dda1da26e5a7c8caac0787a8c7ec3dfec63cc5e6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php');
		}
	}
}
